name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Family Friendly Hot Spring Family Suite
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Family
info:4 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 4, 2023
msg:The rooms in this hotel are very comfortable. The floor height should be 3 meters. The air is very good. The beds are clean and tidy. The decoration is warm and makes people feel at home. I chose the parent-child room. There is a 1.5-meter bed in the lobby outside and a 1.8-meter bed in the room, suitable for 3 people. However, the water flow in the bath is small and the bath is not very "refreshing".
What's more worth mentioning is the hotel's hot spring pool. The water quality of the hot springs here is very clear. Maybe not many people go there during the National Day, and there are not many pools opened, but the hot springs are just right hot, making people feel very comfortable and relaxed.
Maybe because of Evergrande, I feel that many facilities are not well maintained, the surrounding grass is very tall and has not been built, and many fallen leaves have not been cleaned. However, the hotel staff are also very enthusiastic and professional, providing various help and services.
In general, the facilities of this hot spring hotel are very good and new. It can be seen that a lot of money has been invested, but the maintenance cannot keep up. There are few breakfast options, but the overall stay experience is very pleasant.
